\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{RELEASE\ NOTES\ -\/\ VERSION\ 0.6}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{===========================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{Version\ 0.6\ includes\ breaking\ changes\ with\ the\ configuration\ of\ decoders.\ The\ ability\ to\ customize\ the\ number\ of\ output\ channels\ and\ the\ sample\ rate\ has\ been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{removed.\ You\ must\ now\ use\ the\ channel\ count\ and\ sample\ rate\ reported\ by\ the\ MP3\ stream\ itself,\ and\ all\ channel\ and\ sample\ rate\ conversion\ must\ be\ done}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{yourself.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{Changes\ to\ Initialization}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{Previously,\ \`{}drmp3\_init()`,\ etc.\ took\ a\ pointer\ to\ a\ \`{}drmp3\_config`\ object\ that\ allowed\ you\ to\ customize\ the\ output\ channels\ and\ sample\ rate.\ This\ has\ been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{removed.\ If\ you\ need\ the\ old\ behaviour\ you\ will\ need\ to\ convert\ the\ data\ yourself\ or\ just\ not\ upgrade.\ The\ following\ APIs\ have\ changed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}drmp3\_init()`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}drmp3\_init\_memory()`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}drmp3\_init\_file()`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{Miscellaneous\ Changes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{Support\ for\ loading\ a\ file\ from\ a\ \`{}wchar\_t`\ string\ has\ been\ added\ via\ the\ \`{}drmp3\_init\_file\_w()`\ API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{Introducation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{=============}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{dr\_mp3\ is\ a\ single\ file\ library.\ To\ use\ it,\ do\ something\ like\ the\ following\ in\ one\ .c\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}c}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \#define\ DR\_MP3\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \#include\ "{}dr\_mp3.h"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{You\ can\ then\ \#include\ this\ file\ in\ other\ parts\ of\ the\ program\ as\ you\ would\ with\ any\ other\ header\ file.\ To\ decode\ audio\ data,\ do\ something\ like\ the\ following:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}c}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\ mp3;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ if\ (!drmp3\_init\_file(\&mp3,\ "{}MySong.mp3"{},\ NULL))\ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ Failed\ to\ open\ file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_uint64\ framesRead\ =\ drmp3\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32(pMP3,\ framesToRead,\ pFrames);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ drmp3\ object\ is\ transparent\ so\ you\ can\ get\ access\ to\ the\ channel\ count\ and\ sample\ rate\ like\ so:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_uint32\ channels\ =\ mp3.channels;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_uint32\ sampleRate\ =\ mp3.sampleRate;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ example\ above\ initializes\ a\ decoder\ from\ a\ file,\ but\ you\ can\ also\ initialize\ it\ from\ a\ block\ of\ memory\ and\ read\ and\ seek\ callbacks\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{\`{}drmp3\_init\_memory()`\ and\ \`{}drmp3\_init()`\ respectively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{You\ do\ not\ need\ to\ do\ any\ annoying\ memory\ management\ when\ reading\ PCM\ frames\ -\/\ this\ is\ all\ managed\ internally.\ You\ can\ request\ any\ number\ of\ PCM\ frames\ in\ each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{call\ to\ \`{}drmp3\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()`\ and\ it\ will\ return\ as\ many\ PCM\ frames\ as\ it\ can,\ up\ to\ the\ requested\ amount.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{You\ can\ also\ decode\ an\ entire\ file\ in\ one\ go\ with\ \`{}drmp3\_open\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()`,\ \`{}drmp3\_open\_memory\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()`\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{\`{}drmp3\_open\_file\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00460\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00461\ \textcolor{comment}{Calculates\ the\ seekpoints\ based\ on\ PCM\ frames.\ This\ is\ slow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00462\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00463\ \textcolor{comment}{pSeekpoint\ count\ is\ a\ pointer\ to\ a\ uint32\ containing\ the\ seekpoint\ count.\ On\ input\ it\ contains\ the\ desired\ count.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00464\ \textcolor{comment}{On\ output\ it\ contains\ the\ actual\ count.\ The\ reason\ for\ this\ design\ is\ that\ the\ client\ may\ request\ too\ many}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00465\ \textcolor{comment}{seekpoints,\ in\ which\ case\ dr\_mp3\ will\ return\ a\ corrected\ count.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04393\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif\ \ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ dr\_mp3\_c\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04394\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif\ \ }\textcolor{comment}{/*DR\_MP3\_IMPLEMENTATION*/}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04395\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{04396\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04397\ \textcolor{comment}{DIFFERENCES\ BETWEEN\ minimp3\ AND\ dr\_mp3}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04398\ \textcolor{comment}{======================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04399\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ First,\ keep\ in\ mind\ that\ minimp3\ (https://github.com/lieff/minimp3)\ is\ where\ all\ the\ real\ work\ was\ done.\ All\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04400\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ code\ relating\ to\ the\ actual\ decoding\ remains\ mostly\ unmodified,\ apart\ from\ some\ namespacing\ changes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04401\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ dr\_mp3\ adds\ a\ pulling\ style\ API\ which\ allows\ you\ to\ deliver\ raw\ data\ via\ callbacks.\ So,\ rather\ than\ pushing\ data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04402\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ to\ the\ decoder,\ the\ decoder\ \_pulls\_\ data\ from\ your\ callbacks.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04403\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ In\ addition\ to\ callbacks,\ a\ decoder\ can\ be\ initialized\ from\ a\ block\ of\ memory\ and\ a\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04404\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ The\ dr\_mp3\ pull\ API\ reads\ PCM\ frames\ rather\ than\ whole\ MP3\ frames.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04405\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ dr\_mp3\ adds\ convenience\ APIs\ for\ opening\ and\ decoding\ entire\ files\ in\ one\ go.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04406\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ dr\_mp3\ is\ fully\ namespaced,\ including\ the\ implementation\ section,\ which\ is\ more\ suitable\ when\ compiling\ projects}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04407\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ as\ a\ single\ translation\ unit\ (aka\ unity\ builds).\ At\ the\ time\ of\ writing\ this,\ a\ unity\ build\ is\ not\ possible\ when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04408\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ using\ minimp3\ in\ conjunction\ with\ stb\_vorbis.\ dr\_mp3\ addresses\ this.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04409\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04410\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{04411\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04412\ \textcolor{comment}{RELEASE\ NOTES\ -\/\ v0.5.0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04413\ \textcolor{comment}{=======================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04414\ \textcolor{comment}{Version\ 0.5.0\ has\ breaking\ API\ changes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04415\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04416\ \textcolor{comment}{Improved\ Client-\/Defined\ Memory\ Allocation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04417\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04418\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ main\ change\ with\ this\ release\ is\ the\ addition\ of\ a\ more\ flexible\ way\ of\ implementing\ custom\ memory\ allocation\ routines.\ The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04419\ \textcolor{comment}{existing\ system\ of\ DRMP3\_MALLOC,\ DRMP3\_REALLOC\ and\ DRMP3\_FREE\ are\ still\ in\ place\ and\ will\ be\ used\ by\ default\ when\ no\ custom}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04420\ \textcolor{comment}{allocation\ callbacks\ are\ specified.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04421\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04422\ \textcolor{comment}{To\ use\ the\ new\ system,\ you\ pass\ in\ a\ pointer\ to\ a\ drmp3\_allocation\_callbacks\ object\ to\ drmp3\_init()\ and\ family,\ like\ this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04423\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04424\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ void*\ my\_malloc(size\_t\ sz,\ void*\ pUserData)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04425\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04426\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ return\ malloc(sz);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04427\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04428\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ void*\ my\_realloc(void*\ p,\ size\_t\ sz,\ void*\ pUserData)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04429\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04430\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ return\ realloc(p,\ sz);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04431\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04432\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ void\ my\_free(void*\ p,\ void*\ pUserData)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04433\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04434\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ free(p);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04435\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04436\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04437\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04438\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04439\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_allocation\_callbacks\ allocationCallbacks;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04440\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ allocationCallbacks.pUserData\ =\ \&myData;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04441\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ allocationCallbacks.onMalloc\ \ =\ my\_malloc;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04442\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ allocationCallbacks.onRealloc\ =\ my\_realloc;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04443\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ allocationCallbacks.onFree\ \ \ \ =\ my\_free;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04444\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_init\_file(\&mp3,\ "{}my\_file.mp3"{},\ NULL,\ \&allocationCallbacks);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04445\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04446\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ advantage\ of\ this\ new\ system\ is\ that\ it\ allows\ you\ to\ specify\ user\ data\ which\ will\ be\ passed\ in\ to\ the\ allocation\ routines.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04447\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04448\ \textcolor{comment}{Passing\ in\ null\ for\ the\ allocation\ callbacks\ object\ will\ cause\ dr\_mp3\ to\ use\ defaults\ which\ is\ the\ same\ as\ DRMP3\_MALLOC,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04449\ \textcolor{comment}{DRMP3\_REALLOC\ and\ DRMP3\_FREE\ and\ the\ equivalent\ of\ how\ it\ worked\ in\ previous\ versions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04450\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04451\ \textcolor{comment}{Every\ API\ that\ opens\ a\ drmp3\ object\ now\ takes\ this\ extra\ parameter.\ These\ include\ the\ following:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04452\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04453\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_init()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04454\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_init\_file()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04455\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_init\_memory()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04456\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_open\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04457\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_open\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s16()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04458\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_open\_memory\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04459\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_open\_memory\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s16()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04460\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_open\_file\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04461\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_open\_file\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s16()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04462\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04463\ \textcolor{comment}{Renamed\ APIs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04464\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04465\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ following\ APIs\ have\ been\ renamed\ for\ consistency\ with\ other\ dr\_*\ libraries\ and\ to\ make\ it\ clear\ that\ they\ return\ PCM\ frame}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04466\ \textcolor{comment}{counts\ rather\ than\ sample\ counts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04467\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04468\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_open\_and\_read\_f32()\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ drmp3\_open\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04469\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_open\_and\_read\_s16()\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/>\ drmp3\_open\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s16()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04470\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_open\_memory\_and\_read\_f32()\ -\/>\ drmp3\_open\_memory\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04471\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_open\_memory\_and\_read\_s16()\ -\/>\ drmp3\_open\_memory\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s16()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04472\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_open\_file\_and\_read\_f32()\ \ \ -\/>\ drmp3\_open\_file\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04473\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_open\_file\_and\_read\_s16()\ \ \ -\/>\ drmp3\_open\_file\_and\_read\_pcm\_frames\_s16()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04474\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04475\ }
